### Smoothing Techniques Applied to Telugu Bigram Corpus
This file contains smoothed probabilities for each bigram using three techniques:

1. Add-One Smoothing:
   P(w₂ | w₁) = (count(w₁, w₂) + 1) / (count(w₁) + V)
2. Add-K Smoothing (k = 0.3):
   P(w₂ | w₁) = (count(w₁, w₂) + k) / (count(w₁) + k × V)
3. Token Type Smoothing:
   P(w₂ | w₁) = (count(w₁, w₂) + weight(w₂)) / (∑ bigram_counts + ∑ token_type_weights)
